***bukken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bukken.html>bukken</a> (4517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bucken</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bocken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bukken.html>bukken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bukkijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***bul.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a> (42499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bulle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bullo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bulô</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bull</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullen.html>bullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koe.html>koe</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bull <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">male bovine, or one of certain other male mammals</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>surly person</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bull</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stier.html>stier</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullebak.html>bullebak</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bulleboer</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bullenpees</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bulle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bulla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bull, decree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullen.html>bullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>great seal affixed to certain documents, notably <a href = vnd.unilang:charters.html>charters</a> from reigning <a href = vnd.unilang:princes.html>princes</a> and certain dignitaries</li>
<li>such charter</li>
<li>specifically, a papal bull</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullen.html>bullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>trinket, object of little value</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullebak.html>bullebak</a> (17233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullebak.html>bullebak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullebakken.html>bullebakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullebak.html>bullebakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bully</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">jerk</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">churl</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">rude and nasty <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from early 18th c.]</span></li>

***bullock.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a> (15448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bullok</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bulluc</i>, corresponding to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bull</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ock</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boelekijn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullocks.html>bullocks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A young bull.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Newly Translated out of the Originall Tongues: amp; with the Former Translations Diligently Compared and Reuised, by His Maiesties Speciall Comandement. Appointed to be Read in Churches.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="w:King James Version">King James Version</a>), London |  <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barker_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barker (printer)">Robert Barker</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="printer to the Kings Most Excellent Maiestie.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/964384981">964384981</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Leviticus" class="extiw" title="w:Book of Leviticus"><a href = vnd.unilang:leviticus.html>Leviticus</a></a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/1611_Leviticus-Chapter-8/14">8:14</a>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>And he <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></b> for the sin offering: and Aaron and his sons laid their hands upon the head of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></b> for the sin offering.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A castrated bull; an ox.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullocks.html>bullocks</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bullocking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bullocked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To bully.
<ul><li><b>1749</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Fielding, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>Tom</a> Jones</i>, Folio Society 1973, p. 47:
<dl><dd>Yes, you villain, you have defiled my own <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>, you have; and then you have charged <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> with <b>bullocking</b> you into owning the truth.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2017</b>, podcast "Untold <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> The <a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgan.html>Morgan</a> Murder", episode "Master of the Dark <a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>Arts</a>", from minute 11:18
<dl><dd>So you never <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> when you <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gonna.html>gonna</a> fall foul of a furious <b>bullocking</b>. So it became a case of <b>bullocking</b> management, basically. You know, how can I stave off the stress and the bullying for another few days.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullpen.html>bullpen</a> (70727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullpen.html>bullpen</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bullpens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An enclosed area used to hold <a href = vnd.unilang:bulls.html>bulls</a>.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:magnus.html>Magnus</a> and Big Buck are <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> in the <b>bullspen</b>, ready for tonight's <a href = vnd.unilang:rodeo.html>rodeo</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">baseball</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An enclosed area for <a href = vnd.unilang:pitchers.html>pitchers</a> to <a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a> up in during a game.
<dl><dd><i>After that hit, there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> activity in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullpen.html>bullpen</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">baseball</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The relief <a href = vnd.unilang:pitchers.html>pitchers</a> of a team collectively.
<dl><dd><i>Their <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullpen.html>bullpen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> worn out after yesterday's doubleheader where both games <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> 12 <a href = vnd.unilang:innings.html>innings</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A place for someone or something to get ready.
<dl><dd><i>If this team of consultants fails, I have another warming up in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullpen.html>bullpen</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>An open seating arrangement where project <a href = vnd.unilang:teams.html>teams</a> can communicate openly with minimal effort.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> have our sales team in a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullpen.html>bullpen</a></b> setup to keep their energy flowing.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bullseye.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a> (36257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bull's</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eye</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bullseyes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> firearms</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The centre of a target, inside the inner and magpie.</li>
<li>A shot which <a href = vnd.unilang:hits.html>hits</a> the centre of a target.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:darts.html>darts</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The two central rings on a dartboard.</li>
<li>A hard striped peppermint-flavoured boiled sweet.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Thick glass set into the side of a ship to let in light.</li>
<li>A hand-cancelled postmark issued by a counter clerk at a post office, typically done on a receipt for proof of mailing.</li>
<li>The central part of a crown glass disk, with concentric ripple effect.</li>
<li>A convex glass lens which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> placed in front of a <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a> to concentrate the light so as to make it more conspicuous as a signal; also the lantern itself.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1890</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscar_Wilde" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oscar Wilde"><a href = vnd.unilang:oscar.html>Oscar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>Wilde</a></a>,  chapter XII, in  <cite>The Picture of Dorian Gray</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He put on his fur coat and hat and <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> out into the hall. There he paused, hearing the slow heavy tread of the policeman on the pavement outside and seeing the flash of the <b>bull's-eye</b> reflected in the window.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A £50 banknote.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>A cry when someone <a href = vnd.unilang:hits.html>hits</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>bullseye</a></b> of a target.</li>
<li>By extension, a response when someone <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> an accurate statement.
<dl><dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> John steal the petty-cash?" "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:bullseye.html>Bullseye</a></b>"</dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<p>Either from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bult.html>bult</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rug.html>rug</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">back</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or a shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bultrugwalvis</i>.

</p>

***bundel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bundel.html>bundel</a> (26304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bondel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bundil-</i>, derivative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bundą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bundle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bundel.html>bundel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bundels.html>bundels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bundeltje.html>bundeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bundle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verboden.html>verboden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijdschriften.html>tijdschriften</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bundel.html>bundel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gooide.html>gooide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:hans.html>Hans</a> put the illegal <a href = vnd.unilang:magazines.html>magazines</a> together in a <b>bundle</b> and threw them into the fire.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>edition of collected literary works, often poetry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Noura's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bundels.html>bundels</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:essays.html>essays</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verboden.html>verboden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> geconfisceerd <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geheime.html>geheime</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:politie.html>politie</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The essay <b>bundles</b> by Noura <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> banned and confiscated by the secret police.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>any collection of products or services offered together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misschien.html>Misschien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> internet <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:telefoon.html>telefoon</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bundel.html>bundel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Perhaps <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> should choose to buy internet and telephone in a <b>package deal</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bonder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bunra</i>.

</p>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hectare</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An obsolete unit of measurement for <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> area.</li></ol>

***bunzing.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzing</a> (94794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bunsinc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bonsinc</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boesinc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">businc</i>. Further etymology unknown, not found outside the Ingvaeonic language area. Probably a derivative of the dialectal term <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boes</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the now-unproductive <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">originating from, inhabitant of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzing</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunzing.html>bunzinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>European polecat, <i>Mustela putorius</i>

<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">stinkmarter</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ulk</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>visse</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>any polecat in general</li></ol>

</p>

***burcht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:burcht.html>burcht</a> (26760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>With seemingly random addition of <i>-t</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">burch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*burg</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*burg</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*burgz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰerǵʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortified elevation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Burg</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">borough</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-bury</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">burrow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:borg.html>borg</a></i>.
</p><p>For sense two, compare English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">burrow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burcht.html>burcht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burchten.html>burchten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burcht.html>burchtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">citadel</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">castle</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">borough</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">citadel</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kasteel.html>kasteel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterkte.html>sterkte</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">burrow</span> of a badger, fox or beaver</li></ol>

***bureel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bureel.html>bureel</a> (30024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bureel.html>bureel</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">burel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">burel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bureel.html>bureel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burelen.html>burelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bureel.html>bureeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> office

***burger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:burger.html>burger</a> (2887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">burg</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortified city</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burcht.html>burcht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">castle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burger.html>burger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burgers.html>burgers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:burgertje.html>burgertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">burgerin</b>)
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamburger.html>hamburger</a></i>, from the German city <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hamburg</i>, from the name of a fortress in the area, <i>Hammaburg</i>.

***burka.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:burka.html>burka</a> (47679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">बुरक़ा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">burqā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urdu" class="extiw" title="w:Urdu"><a href = vnd.unilang:urdu.html>Urdu</a></a></span> <i class="ur-Arab mention" lang="ur">برقع</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ur-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">burqā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">برقع</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borqa'</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">بُرْقُع</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">burquʿ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:burka.html>burka</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">burkas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An Islamic garment that <a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a> the whole body, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> screen covering the <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> so they cannot be seen, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> worn by women <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also spelled burqa</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>A dress made from felt or karakul (the short <a href = vnd.unilang:curly.html>curly</a> fur of young <a href = vnd.unilang:lambs.html>lambs</a> of the breed of that name), traditionally worn by <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> of the Caucasus region.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Islamic garment</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">paranja</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially in Central Asia</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, chadri</li></ul>
</body>

***burly.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a> (94779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">burely</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">borly</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">burlich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">borlich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">borlic</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tall, stately</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">burely</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rough, <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>stout</a>, sturdy, strong</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">*būrlīċ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noble, stately</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bowerly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bower.html>bower</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ly</i>; or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">*byrlīċ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">high, raised</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">byre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">raised area, mound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">burlīh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">purlīh</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lofty, elevated, high, exalted</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">burjan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to raise, <a href = vnd.unilang:lift.html>lift</a>, push up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <span class="Latn" lang="en">burgeon</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">burlier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">burliest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually of a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Large, well-built, and muscular.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He’s a big, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b> rugby player who works as a landscape gardener.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1841</b> February–November,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="w:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barnaby_Rudge" class="extiw" title="w:Barnaby Rudge">Barnaby Rudge</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Master_Humphrey%27s_Clock" class="extiw" title="w:Master Humphrey | s Clock">Master Humphrey’s Clock</a></cite>, volume II, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chapman_%26_Hall" class="extiw" title="w:Chapman amp; Hall">Chapman amp; Hall</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="186, Strand">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/633494058">633494058</a></small>, chapter 12, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=7j4JAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA301">page 301</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">With no great disparity between them in point of years, they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a>, in every other respect, as unlike and far removed from each other as two <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> could well be. The one <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> soft-spoken, delicately made, precise, and elegant; the other, a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b> square-built <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, negligently dressed, rough and abrupt in manner, stern, and, in his present mood, forbidding both in look and speech.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1914</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louis_Joseph_Vance" class="extiw" title="w:Louis Joseph Vance"><a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Joseph Vance</a>,  chapter III, in  <cite>Nobody</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_H._Doran_Company" class="extiw" title="w:George H. Doran Company">George H[enry] Doran Company</a>, published 1915, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/40817384">40817384</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> frankly disappointed. For some reason she <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> thought to discover a burglar of one or another accepted type—either a dashing cracksman in full-blown evening dress, lithe, polished, pantherish, or a common yegg, a red-eyed, unshaven <b><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:brute.html>brute</a> in the <a href = vnd.unilang:rags.html>rags</a> and tatters of a tramp.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> East End of London<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Great, amazing, unbelievable.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">That goal <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b>.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b> Formula 1 driver.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> surf culture and/or Southern California</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of large magnitude, either good or bad, and sometimes both.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">That wave <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b>! (i.e. large, dangerous and difficult to ride)</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">This hike <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> going to be <b><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b>, but worth it because there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> good body surfing at that beach.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:burl.html>burl</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:burly.html>burly</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Full of burls or <a href = vnd.unilang:knots.html>knots</a>; knotty.</li></ol>

***burrito.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:burrito.html>burrito</a> (19043)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***bus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a> (1105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">omnibus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">omnibus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">for everything/all</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; dative plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">omnis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bussen.html>bussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:busje.html>busje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a></a>, omnibus <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">vehicle</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transport<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:minibus.html>minibus</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:minivan.html>minivan</a></li>
<li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a></a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">electrical conductor</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bussen.html>busse</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bussa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*buhsijǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*buhsuz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Büchse</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">box</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bussen.html>bussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:busje.html>busje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>container, box, tin</li>
<li>bushing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> one of a variety of early modern firearms, such as flintlock and matchlock <a href = vnd.unilang:guns.html>guns</a></li></ol>

***busby.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:busby.html>busby</a> (108412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
Various <a href = vnd.unilang:theories.html>theories</a>; probably from the surname <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:busby.html>Busby</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:busby.html>busby</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">busbies</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">busbys</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fur hat, usually with a plume in the front, worn by certain members of the military or brass <a href = vnd.unilang:bands.html>bands</a>.
<ul><li><b>1895</b>, Robert W. Chambers, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_King_in_Yellow" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The King in Yellow">The King in Yellow</a></i>
